### [107] [Chemical and Kinetic Equilibrium in Cosmology: Facts and Myths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.20988)
*Stefano Profumo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 化学平衡和动力学平衡在早期宇宙中是两个不同的概念，它们的解耦顺序是模型依赖的，且不一定同时发生。文章通过多种物理场景说明了这一点，并强调在宇宙学预测中，当动量选择性重要时，必须考虑相空间演化以获得可靠结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清化学平衡与动力学平衡的区别及其在早期宇宙演化中的不同作用，指出两者解耦顺序的非普适性，以避免在宇宙学建模中出现错误假设。

Method: 通过标准模型中微子解耦、强洗出轻子生成、暗物质多种模型（如共振/禁戒过程、转换/共湮灭、散射）以及具有不同温度的暗区等实例，分析化学与动力学解耦的时序关系，并强调相空间演化的必要性。

Result: 明确了化学平衡控制粒子数密度，动力学平衡控制动量分布形状；二者解耦时间通常不同，顺序取决于具体模型；忽略这一点可能导致不准确的宇宙学预测。

Conclusion: 在早期宇宙研究中，应区分化学和动力学平衡，且在动量分布演化关键的情况下，必须采用相空间演化方法以确保预测的准确性。

Abstract: We clarify that chemical and kinetic equilibration in the early Universe are
distinct: neither implies the other, and the ordering of their decouplings need
not be universal. We illustrate this with Standard-Model neutrino decoupling,
strong-washout leptogenesis, dark-matter scenarios where kinetic decoupling
precedes chemical freeze-out (resonant/forbidden, conversion/coannihilation,
coscattering), and dark sectors at with temperatures distinct from the
visible-sector temperature, with semi-annihilation or 3 $\to$ 2 cannibal
dynamics. The moral of the story is simple: Chemical equilibrium governs
numbers, kinetic equilibrium governs shapes. In an expanding Universe the
operators that control them rarely fade at the same time, and when they do not,
the order of decoupling is model dependent. Turning to phase-space evolution
whenever momentum selectivity matters is the surest way to obtain robust
cosmological predictions.

</details>


### [108] [Baryogenesis via Asymmetric Evaporation of Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.21011)
*Joaquim Iguaz Juan,Yuber F. Perez-Gonzalez,Jessica Turner*

TL;DR: 本文重新研究了轻原始黑洞不对称蒸发中的重子生成，重点关注引力效应引发物质-反物质不对称的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索原始黑洞蒸发过程中重子不对称的产生机制，特别是引力效应如何通过高维算符诱导产生有效化学势。

Method: 引入Kretschmann标量与破坏重子数流的高维算符耦合，考虑蒸发导致的熵稀释、化学势依赖的灰体因子，并数值模拟原始黑洞群体在膨胀宇宙中的完全耦合演化。

Result: 在包括对数正态、临界坍缩和幂律分布等多种原始黑洞质量谱下，参数空间中存在可重现观测到的重子不对称性的可行区域。

Conclusion: 该机制能在合理的参数范围内解释当前观测到的宇宙重子不对称性。

Abstract: We revisit baryogenesis from the asymmetric evaporation of light primordial
black holes, focusing on scenarios where gravitational effects induce a matter
antimatter asymmetry. In particular, we consider a higher-dimension operator
coupling the Kretschmann scalar to a baryon-number-violating current which
generates an effective chemical potential at the black hole horizon and leads
to asymmetric Hawking radiation. Relative to earlier studies, we account for
entropy dilution from evaporation, incorporate chemical potential dependent
greybody factors and numerically track the fully coupled evolution of a PBH
population in an expanding universe. We show that the observed baryon asymmetry
can be reproduced within a viable region of parameter space for several PBH
mass spectra including log-normal, critical-collapse, and power-law
distributions.

</details>


### [109] [Dark Matter-Enhanced Probe of Relic Neutrino Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.21034)
*Writasree Maitra,Anna M. Suliga,Vedran Brdar,P. S. Bhupal Dev*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宇宙中微子背景（CνB）的性质，特别是其局部聚集性，是理解宇宙演化和暗物质性质的关键。现有方法难以直接探测CνB，因此需要新的探针。

Method: 提出重衰变暗物质（质量≳10^9 GeV）衰变为中微子，作为超高能中微子的新来源；结合天体物理和宇宙学中微子流，求解完整的中微子输运方程，考虑吸收和再注入效应，模拟未来中微子望远镜（如IceCube-Gen2 Radio）可观测的能谱。

Result: 发现根据中微子绝对质量、暗物质质量和寿命的不同，IceCube-Gen2 Radio在10年内可探测到局部CνB密度超过10^6倍的过密区域。

Conclusion: 重衰变暗物质为探测CνB提供了一种新途径，未来观测有望揭示CνB的局部结构和暗物质特性。

Abstract: We propose heavy decaying dark matter (DM) as a new probe of the cosmic
neutrino background (C$\nu$B). Heavy DM, with mass $\gtrsim 10^9$ GeV, decaying
into neutrinos can be a new source of ultra-high-energy (UHE) neutrinos.
Including this contribution along with the measured astrophysical and predicted
cosmogenic neutrino fluxes, we study the scattering of UHE neutrinos with the
C$\nu$B via standard weak interactions mediated by the $Z$-boson. We solve the
complete neutrino transport equation, taking into account both absorption and
reinjection effects, to calculate the expected spectrum of UHE neutrino flux at
future neutrino telescopes, such as IceCube-Gen2 Radio. We argue that such
observations can be used to probe the C$\nu$B properties, and in particular,
local C$\nu$B clustering. We find that, depending on the absolute neutrino mass
and the DM mass and lifetime, a local C$\nu$B overdensity $\gtrsim 10^6$ can be
probed at IceCube-Gen2 Radio within 10 years of data taking.

### [110] [A Baryon and Lepton Number Violation Model Testable at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.21064)
*Amit Bhoonah,Francis Burk,Da Liu,Tong Ou,Deepak Sathyan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个新的模型，该模型通过特定的重子数和轻子数破坏模式，允许在远低于大统一能标的低能尺度下存在重子数破坏现象，并预测新粒子质量可达TeV量级，可在LHC和高亮度LHC中探测，同时提出了低能重子生成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统质子衰变实验将重子数破坏限制在大统一能标，使得相关新共振态难以探测；本文旨在探索特定的重子数与轻子数破坏模式，以压制质子衰变，从而允许低能标下的重子数破坏物理。

Method: 构建一个明确的模型，实现ΔB = -1和ΔL = -3的破坏，并结合Super-Kamiokande对p → e⁺/μ⁺ν̄ν̄衰变模式的限制，分析新粒子的质量尺度及其在LHC上的可探测性。

Result: 模型中新引入的基本粒子质量可达TeV量级，尽管受到Super-Kamiokande实验的严格限制；该模型具有独特的重子数破坏信号，可在当前和未来的LHC实验中探测，并提出了低能重子生成方案。

Conclusion: 特定的重子数与轻子数破坏模式可显著压制质子衰变，使重子数破坏物理可能出现在TeV能标，为LHC等实验提供了可检验的新物理信号，并支持低能重子生成机制。

Abstract: Proton decay experiments typically constrain baryon number violation to the
scale of grand unified theories. From a phenomenological point of view, this
makes direct probing of the associated new resonances, such as the X and Y
bosons, out of reach for even the most optimistic future experiments. It has,
however, been known that certain specific patterns of baryon and lepton number
violation can suppress proton decay by multiple powers of the masses of the
heavy resonances involved, opening the possibility that the observed limits on
the proton lifetime are consistent with baryon number violating physics at
energy scales much lower than that of grand unification. We construct an
explicit example of such a model which violates baryon number by one unit,
$\Delta \text{B} = -1$, and lepton number by three units, $\Delta \text{L} =
-3$, and show that despite stringent limits on the predicted $p \rightarrow
e^{+}/\mu^{+} \overline{\nu}\overline{\nu}$ mode from the Super-Kamiokande
experiment, the masses of the newly introduced elementary particles can be
$\mathcal{O}$(TeV). We identify interesting unique signatures of baryon number
violation of this model that can be probed both with currently available LHC
data and with the upcoming High-Luminosity LHC. We also present a scenario for
low-scale baryogenesis within the framework of this model.

</details>

### [111] [Empirical investigation of nuclear correlation function distributions in lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.20378)
*William Detmold,Rohan Kanchana,Cagin Yunus*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 研究了不同重子数下格点QCD中两点关联函数的经验分布，并发现O(N)模型的理论分布能准确描述这些分布，尤其是在大时间分离时，QCD关联函数的行为与O(N ~ 2/B)模型分布吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索格点QCD中重子数相关两点关联函数的经验分布特性，并验证是否可用简单理论模型（如O(N)模型）来描述这些复杂系统的行为。

Method: 使用格点QCD计算B ∈ {1,2,3,4}的两点关联函数，分析蒙特卡洛重要性抽样样本的经验分布随时空分离和重子数的变化，并通过多种统计检验将其与O(N)模型的渐近理论分布进行比较。

Result: O(N)模型的理论分布在零动量下能准确描述各重子数的QCD关联函数经验分布，且在大时间分离时，B重子数的QCD关联函数行为与O(N ~ 2/B)模型分布高度一致。

Conclusion: O(N)模型为理解格点QCD中多体强相互作用系统的关联函数统计行为提供了有效的理论框架，表明某些复杂QCD现象可通过更简单的无序场论模型来刻画。

Abstract: Two-point correlation functions of systems with baryon number $B \in
\{1,2,3,4\}$ are investigated using lattice Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD). In
particular, the empirical distributions of importance-sampling Monte-Carlo
samples of these correlation functions are examined as a function of the
spacetime separation between the two points and the baryon number. While the
exact forms of these distributions are not known for QCD, recent work has
determined asymptotic expressions for analogous correlation function
distributions in simpler theories such as scalar field theory and the
disordered phase of the $O(N)$ model. The theoretical O(N) model distributions
are found to provide an accurate description of the empirical QCD distributions
at zero momentum over a wide range of temporal separations for each baryon
number when assessed with a range of different statistical tests. In
particular, the behaviour of the baryon number $B$ QCD correlation function at
large temporal separation is well-reproduced by the $O(N \sim 2/B)$ model
distribution.

### [112] [Studying Effective String Theory using deep generative models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.20610)
*Michele Caselle,Elia Cellini,Alessandro Nada*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文介绍了有效弦理论（EST）及其在描述杨-米尔斯理论中禁闭现象的应用，特别是通过将静态夸克-反夸克对之间的禁闭通量管视为细长振动弦。虽然EST通常使用zeta函数正则化进行计算，但某些问题（如确定通量管宽度）难以解析求解。最近的研究表明，可以通过基于生成算法的深度学习技术对EST进行数值探索。本文简要介绍了EST和这种新颖的数值方法，并展示了Nambu-Gotō EST通量管宽度的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决有效弦理论中难以解析求解的问题，如通量管宽度的计算，探索新的数值方法。

Method: 采用基于深度学习的生成算法对有效弦理论进行数值模拟。

Result: 成功计算了Nambu-Gotō有效弦理论中通量管的宽度。

Conclusion: 深度学习方法为研究有效弦理论提供了可行的数值途径，特别是在解析方法受限的情况下。

Abstract: Effective String Theory (EST) offers a robust non-perturbative framework for
describing confinement in Yang-Mills theory by treating the confining flux tube
between a static quark-antiquark pair as a thin, vibrating string. While EST
calculations are typically carried out using zeta-function regularization,
certain problems-such as determining the flux tube width-are too complex to
solve analytically. However, recent studies have demonstrated that EST can be
explored numerically by employing deep learning techniques based on generative
algorithms. In this work, we provide a brief introduction to EST and this novel
numerical approach. Finally, we present results for the width of the
Nambu-Got\"o EST.

</details>
